function createCookie(name,value,days) { if (days) {
var date = new Date();
date.setTime(date.getTime()+(days*24*60*60*1000));
var expires = "; expires="+date.toGMTString();
}
else var expires = "";
document.cookie = name+"="+value+expires+"; path=/";
}
function eraseCookie(name) {
createCookie(name,"",-1);
}
function readCookie(name) {
var nameEQ = name + "=";
var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
for(var i=0;i < ca.length;i++) {
var c = ca[i];
while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1,c.length);
if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length);
}
return null;
}
function deleteCookie(name) {
createCookiewithdomain(name,null,-1);
}
function createCookiewithdomain(name,value,days) {
if (days) {
var date = new Date();
date.setTime(date.getTime()+(days*24*60*60*1000));
var expires = "; expires="+date.toGMTString();
}
else var expires = "";
document.cookie = name+"="+value+expires+"; domain="+document.location.host.match(/\.[.\w]*/)+";path=/";
}
function getStorage(name){	if(typeof(Storage) !== "undefined" && 'localStorage' in window && window.localStorage !== null) {	if (localStorage.getItem(name)){	cookieObj = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(name));
if (cookieObj !== undefined && (cookieObj.e == null || cookieObj.e > new Date())){return cookieObj.v === undefined ? null : cookieObj.v ; }	else{localStorage.removeItem(name);}	}
return null;	} else {return readCookie(name);}	}
function setStorage(name,value,days){
if(typeof(Storage) !== "undefined" && 'localStorage' in window && window.localStorage !== null) {
var date = new Date();	localStorage.setItem(name,JSON.stringify({"v":value, "e":date.setTime(date.getTime()+(days*24*60*60*1000))}))
} else {createCookie(name,value,days);}	}
function eraseStorage(name){ if(typeof(Storage) !== "undefined" && 'localStorage' in window && window.localStorage !== null) {localStorage.removeItem(name);}
else{eraseCookie(name)}
}
function getUrlParameter( name, url ) {
if (!url) url = location.href;
name = name.replace(/[\[]/,"\\\[").replace(/[\]]/,"\\\]");
var regexS = "[\\?&]"+name+"=([^&#]*)";
var regex = new RegExp(regexS,"i");
var results = regex.exec( url );
return results == null ? null : results[1];
}

function loadPromiseScript(src) {
return new Promise(function(resolve, reject) {
let script = document.createElement('script');
script.src = src;
script.async = true;
script.onload = function(){
resolve(script);
}
document.head.append(script);
});
}
function crossfetchGet(url,fn){
// Default options are marked with *
return fetch(url, {
method: 'GET', // *GET, POST, PUT, DELETE, etc.
mode: 'cors', // no-cors, cors, *same-origin
credentials: 'include', // include, *same-origin, omit
}).then(function(response) {
if(response.ok) {
return response.json();
}
else{
return Promise.reject();
throw new Error('Network response was not ok.' + url + "-"+ response.statusText);
}
}).then(function(respone) {
fn(respone);
}).catch(function(error) {
return Promise.reject();
throw new Error(error.message);
});
}	function crossfetchPost(url, data, fn) {
return fetch(url, {
method: 'POST',
body: JSON.stringify(data),
mode: 'cors', // no-cors, cors, *same-origin
credentials: 'include', // include, *same-origin, omit
}).then(function(response) {
if(response.ok) {
return response.json();
}
else{
return Promise.resolve();
throw new Error('Network response was not ok.' + url + "-"+ response.statusText);
}
}).then(function(respone) {
fn(respone);
}).catch(function(error) {
return Promise.resolve();
throw new Error(error.message);
});
}
function fetchtimeout(ms,url,options,fn) {
const FETCH_TIMEOUT = ms;
let didTimeOut = false;
return new Promise(function(resolve, reject) {
const timeout = setTimeout(function() {
didTimeOut = true;
reject(new Error('Request timed out -> ' +ms +" ms"));
}, FETCH_TIMEOUT);
fetch(url,options).then(function(response) {
// Clear the timeout as cleanup
clearTimeout(timeout);
if(!didTimeOut) {
resolve(response);
}
})
.catch(function(err) {
// Rejection already happened with setTimeout
if(didTimeOut) return;
// Reject with error
reject(err);
//	console.error(err.message +"= "+url);
})
}).then(function(response) {
// Request success and no timeout
if(response.ok) {
return response.json();
}
else
{
console.error('Network response was not ok.' + url + "-"+ response.statusText); }
})
.then(function(response) {
fn(response);
})
.catch(function(err) {
// Error: response error, request timeout or runtime error
console.error(err.message +"= "+url);
return Promise.resolve();
//return Promise.reject();
})
}
function fetchApi(url,options,fn) {
return fetch(url,options).then(function(response) {
if(response.ok) {
return response.json();
}
else{
return Promise.resolve();
throw new Error('Network response was not ok.' + url + "-"+ response.statusText);
}
}).then(function(respone) {
fn(respone);
}).catch(function(error) {
return Promise.resolve();
throw new Error(error.message);
});
}

         <script>
          function dateformat(){
var toDayDate;
var days = ['Sunday','Monday','Tuesday','Wednesday','Thursday','Friday','Saturday'];
var months = ['January','February','March','April','May','June','July','August','September','October','November','December'];
var today = new Date();
var day = days[ today.getDay() ];
var month = months[ today.getMonth() ];
toDayDate = day + ", " + month +" " + today.getDate() + ", " + today.getFullYear();
return toDayDate;
}
$(function(){
$("#todaysdate").html(dateformat());
});

document.getElementsByClassName("subsEntrymenu").length > 0 ? document.getElementsByClassName("subsEntrymenu")[0].style.display = "block" : '';
document.getElementsByClassName("submobileentry").length > 0 ? document.getElementsByClassName("submobileentry")[0].style.display = "block" : '';
}
tp.pianoId.init({
loggedIn : function(data) {
thgloggedIn(data)
},
loggedOut: function() {
console.log('user logged out');
},
profileUpdate : function(data) {
typeof __thg_event != "undefined" ? __thg_event.triggerProfileupdate(data): null;
}
});
}]);
function thgloggedIn(data) {
isUserDetails = data;
var userName = typeof tp.pianoId.getUser().firstName != "undefined" ? "Hi " + tp.pianoId.getUser().firstName : 'Hi User';
document.getElementById("sso-signin") != null ? document.getElementById("sso-signin").innerText = userName :'';
document.getElementById("sso-signin") != null ? document.getElementById("sso-signin").classList.remove("thgsignin"):'';
document.getElementById("mobilesignin") != null ? document.getElementById("mobilesignin").classList.remove("sso-signin"):'';
document.getElementById("mobilesignin") != null ? document.getElementById("mobilesignin").classList.add("sso-signinmobile"):'';
document.getElementById("mobilesigninlink") != null ? document.getElementById("mobilesigninlink").classList.remove("thgsignin"):'';
if(DevIdf.isMobile == true){
var dropdown = '<ul class="dropdown-menu sso-signinuser mobileThsubscrip">'
+ '<li class="mobileusername" ><i class="fa fa-user"></i><a class="" >'
+ userName
+ '</a>'
+ tp.pianoId.getUser().email
+ '<li class="Subscribebtnremove" data-category="Hi user" data-label="SUBSCRIBE NOW"><a class="Subscribebtn" href="/subscription/">Subscribe Now</a>'
+ '<li data-category="Hi user" data-label="My Dashboard"><a href="/my-dashboard/" class="sso-profile">My Dashboard</a></li>'
+ '<li data-category="Hi user" data-label="My Account"><a href="/myaccount/" class="sso-profile">My Account</a>'
+ '<li data-category="Hi user" data-label="FAQ"><a href="/faq/" target="_blank" class="sso-profile">FAQS</a></li>'
+'<li data-category="Hi user" data-label="Contact us"><a href="/contacts/" target="_blank" class="sso-profile">Contact Us</a></li>'
+ '<li data-category="Hi user" data-label="Sign Out"><a class="sso-logout" onclick="thgLogout();" >Sign Out</a>'
+ '</ul>';
}else {
var dropdown = '<ul class="dropdown-menu sso-signinuser">'
+ '<li class="mobileusername" ><a class="" >'
+ userName
+ '</a>'
+ '<li data-category="Hi user" data-label="My Dashboard"><a href="/my-dashboard/" class="sso-profile">My Dashboard</a></li>'
+ '<li data-category="Hi user" data-label="My Account"><a href="/myaccount/" class="sso-profile">My Account</a>'
+ '<li data-category="Hi user" data-label="FAQ"><a href="/faq/" target="_blank" class="sso-profile">FAQS</a></li>'
+'<li data-category="Hi user" data-label="Contact us"><a href="/contacts/" target="_blank" class="sso-profile">Contact Us</a></li>'
+ '<li data-category="Hi user" data-label="Sign Out"><a class="sso-logout" onclick="thgLogout();" >Sign Out</a>'
+ '</ul>';
}
var list = document.querySelectorAll(".signinbtn");
for (var i = 0; i < list.length; ++i) {
list[i].classList.remove('subscribeBtnCss');
list[i].classList.add('ssologin');
list[i].insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend', dropdown);
}
var listmobile = document.querySelectorAll(".sigininmobile");
for (var i = 0; i < listmobile.length; ++i) {
listmobile[i].insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend', dropdown);
}
document.getElementsByClassName("subsEntrymenu").length > 0 ? document.getElementsByClassName("subsEntrymenu")[0].style.display = "block" : '';
document.getElementsByClassName("submobileentry").length > 0 ? document.getElementsByClassName("submobileentry")[0].style.display = "block" : '';
}

function thgLogout() {
typeof __thg_event != "undefined" ? __thg_event.triggerLogOut(tp.pianoId.getUser()): null;
tp.push(["init", function () {
tp = window.tp || [];
tp.pianoId.logout()
location.reload();
}]);
}

           <script>
            var emailAddressFilter = /^([\w-]+(?:\.[\w-]+)*)@((?:[\w-]+\.)*\w[\w-]{0,66})\.([a-z]{2,6}(?:\.[a-z]{2})?)$/;
function validate_email(fieldId) {
var email = $(fieldId).val();
email= email.trim();
if (email == "" || email == "undefined") {
return false;
} else if (!emailAddressFilter.test(email)) {
return false;
}
return true;
}
<!-- article page contains multiple times if infinite scroll is enabled. -->
$(document).ready(function(){
$(".newsletter-container button.nl-submit:last").on("click", function(event){
$(this).attr("disabled","disabled");
var selector = $(this).closest(".newsletter");
$(selector).find("input").click(function(){$(selector).find("button").removeAttr("disabled");});
var email = $(selector).find("input").val();
email= email.trim();
$(selector).find(".nl-error").css("display", "none");
$(selector).find(".nl-success").css("display", "block");
$(selector).find("input").removeClass("error");
if (validate_email($(selector).find("input"))){
$(selector).find(".nl-load").show();
$(selector).find(".nl-load").addClass("active");
var url = publist("url") + 's/mailsubscription/subscribeNlDirect/';
var data = {"email" : email,"category" : "newsletter"};
var s = fetchPost(url,data);
s.then(function(result) {
$(selector).find(".nl-load").hide();
document.getElementById("demo").innerHTML=result.data;
});
} else {
$(selector).find(".nl-load").fadeOut( "slow");
$(selector).find(".nl-error").css("display", "block");
$(selector).find(".nl-success").css("display", "none");
$(selector).find("input").addClass("error");
}
});
});
           </script>

   <script data-cfasync="false">
    async function eagerLoading(){
var sizes = imageSizes;
var imgSelector = "img.adaptive.lazy";
var position = 0;
for ( var type in WFClientTypeDef) {
if (window.matchMedia(WFClientTypeDef[type]).matches) {
switch (type) {
case "xlarge":
position = 0;
break;
case "large":
position = 1;
break;
case "medium":
position = 2;
break;
case "small":
position = 3;
break;
}
break;
}
}
var elements = document.querySelectorAll(imgSelector);
Array.prototype.slice.call(elements).slice(0,2).forEach(function(el, i){	var template = el.getAttribute('data-src-template');
if (template == null) {
return;
}
var prevWidth = el.getAttribute('data-selected-width');
if (prevWidth !== null) {
return;
}
var variant = el.getAttribute('data-variant');
var customVariant = variant+"~"+el.getAttribute('data-device-variant');
if("" != el.getAttribute('data-device-variant'))
variant = customVariant.split("~")[position];	var elementWidth = el.offsetWidth;
var selected = Math.max.apply(null, sizes);
for (var i = 0; i < sizes.length; i++) {
if (elementWidth <= sizes[i]) {
selected = sizes[i];
break;
}
} if (prevWidth && prevWidth >= selected) {
return;
}	el.setAttribute('data-selected-width',selected);
var binaryRegEx = new RegExp("binary", "ig");
var thumbnailRegEx = new RegExp("thumbnail", "ig");
var adaptedSrc = template.replace(binaryRegEx, "alternates").replace(thumbnailRegEx, variant + "_" + selected);
el.setAttribute('src',appURL() + "static/img/placeholder/" + variant + ".gif"); el.setAttribute('src', adaptedSrc);	}
);
}	if(typeof(eagerLoading) == 'function'){eagerLoading();}
   </script>

          userIdentify.then(function() {

googletag.cmd.push(function() { googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-1521709628297-6'); });
}
else if(isDeviceEnabled("[medium, small]") && !isNonSubcribedUser()){
$(document).ready(function () {
adfiller.push({"selector":'div-gpt-ad-1521709628297-6',"type":"edit"});
});
}
});
         </script>
        </div>

  <script>
   $(document).ready(function (e) {
$(document).on("makeSocialShareReady", function(event, data) {
var selector = $(data).find(".hover-social-media-top ul li, .hover-social-media-bottom ul li");
$(selector).on('click', function (e) {
var shareUrl = $(this).parents('[data-share-url]').data('share-url');
var shareText = $(this).parents('[data-share-url]').data('share-text');
var shareValue ="";
if ($(this).find('i').hasClass('fa-facebook')) {
shareValue = "facebook";
openShareLink('http://www.facebook.com/sharer/sharer.php?u=' + encodeURIComponent(shareUrl));
} else if ($(this).find('i').hasClass('fa-twitter')) {
shareValue = "twitter";
openShareLink('http://twitter.com/share?text=' + encodeURIComponent(shareText) + '&url=' + encodeURIComponent(shareUrl));
}
});
});
$(document).on('pageContentReady', function (event, content) {
$(document).trigger( "makeSocialShareReady", content );
});
});
$(document).ready(function (e) {
$(document).trigger( "makeSocialShareReady", $('body') );
});
function openShareLink(pLink) {
var popUp = window.open(pLink, 'popupwindow', 'scrollbars=yes,width=740,height=400');
popUp.focus();
return false;
}
  </script>

  <script>
   $(document).ready(function () {
var url1 = "https://www.thehindu.com/news/states/";
getGeoContent(url1, "14268388", "#geoStatesArt");
var url2 = "https://www.thehindu.com/news/cities/";
getGeoContent(url2, "14269771", "#geoCitiesArt");
$(".geo-states .shp-list").on("click", "li", function(e){
geoMenuClickHandler($(this), "14269051", "#geoStatesArt",
".geo-statesLabel", ".geo-states");
});
$(".geo-cities .shp-list").on("click", "li", function(e){
geoMenuClickHandler($(this), "14269152", "#geoCitiesArt",
".geo-citiesLabel", ".geo-cities");
});
});
function geoMenuClickHandler(obj, sectionParam, targetSelector, geoLabelSelector, contextSelector){
var geoUrl = obj.find("a").attr("data-section-url");
var label = obj.find("a").text();
getGeoContent(geoUrl, sectionParam, targetSelector);
updateGeoLabel(geoLabelSelector, geoUrl, label);
$(contextSelector).find("a.open-button").toggleClass('focus').toggleClass('above-dropdown');
$(contextSelector).find(".section-header-popup").toggleClass("is-show").toggleClass("dropdown-top");
obj.parent().find("a").removeClass("active");
obj.find("a").addClass("active");
$(".overlay-screen").toggleClass("is-visible");
}
function getGeoContent(geoUrl, widgetId, targetSelector) {
// common method to fetch geo content
var geoPromise = $.ajax({
url: geoUrl + "?service=widget&widgetContentId=" + widgetId + "&widgetName=widget_magic"
});
geoPromise.done(function (r) {
var content = $("<div class='lazy-on-demand'>").html(r);
$(targetSelector).html(content)
$.event.trigger('pageContentReady', content);
});
}
function updateGeoLabel(selector, url, label) {
$(selector).attr("href", url).html(label);
}
  </script>

  </div>
